  <a id="5743" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="5745" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5745" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="5748" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5748" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="5751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5753" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5760" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5761" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5761" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5765" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5768" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5745" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="5770" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5773" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5773" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5777" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.circle.html#1083" class="Function">free-loop</a> <a id="5787" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5761" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5788" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5790" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="5794" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5796" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5796" class="Bound">dup-circle</a> <a id="5807" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5809" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.circle.html#6031" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-circle</a> <a id="5845" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5748" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="5848" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5773" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5849" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5851" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="5855" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5857" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5857" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="5859" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5861" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5761" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5863" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5865" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5868" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5748" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="5870" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5872" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5873" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5873" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="5875" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5877" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#1472" class="Function">Fam-circle</a> <a id="5888" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5748" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="5890" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5892" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="5896" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5898" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5898" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5900" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5902" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#1547" class="Function">Eq-Fam-circle</a> <a id="5916" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5873" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="5918" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5919" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#2885" class="Function">ev-fam-circle</a> <a id="5933" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5773" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5935" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5857" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="5936" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5939" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="5943" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5206" class="Function">Section-Fam-circle</a> <a id="5962" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5773" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5964" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5873" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="5966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5968" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5969" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5969" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5971" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5973" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5761" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5974" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5976" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5978" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5857" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="5980" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5969" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="5982" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#5720" class="Function">section-fam-circle</a> <a id="6001" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6001" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6003" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6003" class="Bound">dup-circle</a> <a id="6014" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6014" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="6016" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6016" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6019" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#575" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="6024" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6024" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="6026" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6026" class="Bound">H</a><a id="6027" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6029" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6030" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#575" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="6035" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6035" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="6037" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6037" class="Bound">α</a><a id="6038" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6040" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="6044" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#4173" class="Function">map-inv-is-equiv</a>
    <a id="6065" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6067" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6003" class="Bound">dup-circle</a> <a id="6078" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6014" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="6079" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6085" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6087" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#575" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="6092" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6093" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="6103" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6024" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="6105" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6035" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6106" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6108" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="6110" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1552" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="6114" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6115" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6026" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="6117" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6035" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6118" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6121" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1239" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="6123" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6124" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="6127" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6128" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="6138" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6024" class="Bound">e</a><a id="6139" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6141" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#6037" class="Bound">α</a><a id="6142" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="6147" class="Comment">{- Section 12.2 The fundamental cover of the circle -}</a>

<a id="6203" class="Comment">{- We show that if a type with a free loop satisfies the induction principle
   of the circle with respect to any universe level, then it satisfies the
   induction principle with respect to the zeroth universe level. -}</a>

<a id="11645" class="Comment">{- We show that the fundamental cover of the circle is a family of sets. -}</a>

              <a id="19722" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19724" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19726" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#14265" class="Function">equiv-contraction-total-space</a> <a id="19756" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18760" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19758" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18763" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19760" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18780" class="Bound">e&#39;</a><a id="19762" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19764" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7855" class="Function Operator">∘e</a>
                <a id="19783" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19785" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5707" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="19795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19796" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#14265" class="Function">equiv-contraction-total-space</a> <a id="19826" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18760" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19828" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18763" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19830" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18780" class="Bound">e&#39;</a><a id="19832" class="Symbol">))))</a>
            <a id="19849" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19851" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18787" class="Bound">h&#39;</a><a id="19853" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="19857" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7855" class="Function Operator">∘e</a>
        <a id="19868" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19870" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#16732" class="Function">equiv-ap</a>
          <a id="19889" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19891" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19893" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#13757" class="Function">equiv-tr-contraction-total-space&#39;</a> <a id="19927" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18760" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19929" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#694" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="19934" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18776" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19936" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18778" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="19938" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18780" class="Bound">e&#39;</a> <a id="19941" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18783" class="Bound">H</a><a id="19942" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19944" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7855" class="Function Operator">∘e</a>
            <a id="19959" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19961" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#14265" class="Function">equiv-contraction-total-space</a> <a id="19991" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18760" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19993" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18763" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19995" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18780" class="Bound">e&#39;</a><a id="19997" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="20010" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20012" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5022" class="Function">map-inv-equiv</a> <a id="20026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20027" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#14265" class="Function">equiv-contraction-total-space</a> <a id="20057" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18760" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20059" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18763" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20061" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18778" class="Bound">e</a><a id="20062" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20064" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18785" class="Bound">h</a><a id="20065" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="20077" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20079" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5022" class="Function">map-inv-equiv</a> <a id="20093" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20094" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#14265" class="Function">equiv-contraction-total-space</a> <a id="20124" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18760" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20126" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18763" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20128" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18780" class="Bound">e&#39;</a><a id="20130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20132" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#18787" class="Bound">h&#39;</a><a id="20134" class="Symbol">)))))</a>

<a id="20141" class="Comment">{- We use the above construction to provide sufficient conditions for the total
   space of the fundamental cover to be contractible. -}</a>

      <a id="26507" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26509" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26510" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26510" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="26512" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26514" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1867" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="26515" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26517" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26519" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="26522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26523" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26469" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26526" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3458" class="Function">succ-ℤ</a> <a id="26533" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26510" class="Bound">k</a><a id="26534" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="26537" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="26539" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="26549" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26550" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26440" class="Bound">pS</a> <a id="26553" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26510" class="Bound">k</a><a id="26554" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="26557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26558" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26469" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26560" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26510" class="Bound">k</a><a id="26561" class="Symbol">)))))</a>

  <a id="28501" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28503" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28503" class="Bound">p0</a> <a id="28506" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28508" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28482" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28510" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2119" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a><a id="28516" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28519" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28519" class="Bound">pS</a> <a id="28522" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28525" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28525" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="28527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28529" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1867" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="28530" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28532" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28534" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28535" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28482" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28537" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28525" class="Bound">k</a><a id="28538" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28540" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="28542" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28543" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28482" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28546" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3458" class="Function">succ-ℤ</a> <a id="28553" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28525" class="Bound">k</a><a id="28554" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28558" class="Symbol">→</a>

              <a id="29901" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29903" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="29905" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#29905" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="29907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29909" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#29905" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="29911" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#467" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="29913" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29914" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="29918" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29919" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="29923" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#28935" class="Bound">s</a><a id="29924" class="Symbol">))))</a>

  <a id="30590" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30592" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30592" class="Bound">p0</a> <a id="30595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30597" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30571" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30599" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2119" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a><a id="30605" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30607" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30608" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30608" class="Bound">pS</a> <a id="30611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30613" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30614" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30614" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="30616" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30618" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1867" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="30619" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30621" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30624" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30571" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30626" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30614" class="Bound">k</a><a id="30627" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30629" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="30631" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30632" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30571" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30634" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30635" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3458" class="Function">succ-ℤ</a> <a id="30642" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#30614" class="Bound">k</a><a id="30643" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="30647" class="Symbol">→</a>

        <a id="31052" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31054" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#26569" class="Function">Elim-ℤ</a>

<a id="31535" class="Comment">-- The universal property of ℤ is now just a special case</a>

<a id="ELIM-ℤ&#39;"></a><a id="31594" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31594" class="Function">ELIM-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="31602" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="31606" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="31608" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31608" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="31611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31613" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="31618" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31620" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31621" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31621" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="31623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31625" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="31628" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31608" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="31630" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31633" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31633" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31635" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31637" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31621" class="Bound">X</a><a id="31638" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31641" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31641" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="31643" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31645" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31621" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="31647" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="31649" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31621" class="Bound">X</a><a id="31650" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31652" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31654" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="31657" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-cover-circle.html#31608" class="Bound">l1</a>
